DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  # Set environment variables
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Rust toolchain
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  # Install cargo extensions
  RUN cargo install \
      cargo-deny \
      cargo-release \
      cargo-typos \
      pre-commit \
      renovate
  # Create and set working directory
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  # Copy only the files needed for dependency resolution first
  COPY Cargo.toml Cargo.lock ./
  # Install dependencies
  RUN cargo fetch
  # Copy remaining files
  COPY . .
  # Configure x86_64 settings
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  # Build the project
  RUN cargo build --features debug && \
      cargo test --no-run
  # Set up development environment
  RUN pre-commit install && \
      cargo typos --write-changes && \
      cargo deny check
  # Verify installation
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  RUN cargo install cargo-deny --locked && \
      cargo install cargo-release --locked && \
      cargo install cargo-typos --locked && \
      cargo install pre-commit --locked && \
      cargo install renovate --locked
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY Cargo.toml Cargo.lock ./
  RUN cargo fetch
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo build --features debug && \
      cargo test --no-run
  RUN pre-commit install && \
      cargo typos --write-changes && \
      cargo deny check
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo fetch --locked
  RUN cargo build --verbose
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo fetch --locked
  RUN cargo build --verbose || (echo "Build failed, showing backtrace:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=1 cargo build --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo fetch --locked
  RUN cargo check --verbose || (echo "Dependency check failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=1 cargo check --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo build --verbose || (echo "Build failed, showing backtrace:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose || (echo "Test compilation failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile
  RUN cargo update
  RUN cargo fetch --locked --verbose
  RUN cargo check --verbose --frozen || (echo "Dependency check failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo build --verbose || (echo "Build failed, showing backtrace:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose || (echo "Test compilation failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile
  RUN cargo update --verbose
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose
  RUN cargo check --verbose || (echo "Dependency check failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo build --verbose || (echo "Build failed, showing backtrace:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose || (echo "Test compilation failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose && exit 1)
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 11 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      cargo update --verbose && \
      cargo fetch --verbose && \
      cargo check --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      (echo "Dependency check failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" && exit 1)
  RUN cargo build --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      (echo "Build failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" && exit 1)
  RUN cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      (echo "Test compilation failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" && exit 1)
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \

      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      echo "Lockfile generated successfully"
  RUN cargo update --verbose && \
      echo "Cargo update completed successfully"
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose && \
      echo "Dependencies fetched successfully"
  RUN cargo check --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" && \
      echo "Dependency check completed successfully" || \

      (echo "Build failed:" && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" && exit 1)

      echo "Test compilation completed successfully" || \

  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  COPY . .

      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      echo "Lockfile generated successfully"
  RUN cargo update --verbose && \
      echo "Cargo update completed successfully"
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose && \
      echo "Dependencies fetched successfully"
  RUN echo "Starting cargo check..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      (echo "Cargo check failed with features 'derive', trying without features..." && \
       RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets
  RUN RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets --features "derive" || \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      echo "Lockfile generated successfully"
  RUN cargo update --verbose && \
      echo "Cargo update completed successfully"
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose && \
      echo "Dependencies fetched successfully"
  RUN echo "Checking workspace members individually..."
  RUN for member in clap_builder clap_derive clap_complete clap_complete_nushell clap_lex clap_mangen; do \
      echo "Checking $member..." && \
      (cd $member && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets) || exit 1; \
      done
  RUN echo "Building workspace members individually..."
  RUN for member in clap_builder clap_derive clap_complete clap_complete_nushell clap_lex clap_mangen; do \
      echo "Building $member..." && \
      (cd $member && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets) || exit 1; \
      done
  RUN echo "Testing workspace members individually..."
  RUN for member in clap_builder clap_derive clap_complete clap_complete_nushell clap_lex clap_mangen; do \
      echo "Testing $member..." && \
      (cd $member && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets) || exit 1; \
      done
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      echo "Lockfile generated successfully"
  RUN cargo update --verbose && \
      echo "Cargo update completed successfully"
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose && \
      echo "Dependencies fetched successfully"
  RUN echo "Checking clap_builder..." && \
      (cd clap_builder && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Checking clap_derive..." && \
      (cd clap_derive && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Checking clap_complete..." && \
      (cd clap_complete && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Checking clap_complete_nushell..." && \
      (cd clap_complete_nushell && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Checking clap_lex..." && \
      (cd clap_lex && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Checking clap_mangen..." && \
      (cd clap_mangen && RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo check --verbose --all-targets)
  RUN echo "Building workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets
  RUN echo "Testing workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \

      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile
  RUN cargo update --verbose
  RUN cargo fetch --verbose
  RUN echo "Building workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --all-targets
  RUN echo "Testing workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --all-targets
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM rust:1.74-slim-bullseye
  ENV CARGO_BUILD_JOBS=$(nproc) \
      RUSTUP_HOME=/usr/local/rustup \
      CARGO_HOME=/usr/local/cargo \
      PATH=/usr/local/cargo/bin:$PATH \
      STABLE=1.89 \
      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      cargo update --verbose && \
      cargo fetch --verbose
  RUN echo "Building workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --workspace --all-targets --frozen
  RUN echo "Testing workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --workspace --all-targets --frozen
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      git \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN rustup toolchain install stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup default stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy && \
      rustup target add wasm32-unknown-unknown --toolchain stable-x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu
  WORKDIR /clap-rs_clap
  COPY . .
  RUN mkdir -p .cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "cc"' > .cargo/config.toml
  RUN cargo generate-lockfile && \
      cargo update --verbose && \
      cargo fetch --verbose
  RUN echo "Building workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo build --verbose --workspace --all-targets
  RUN echo "Testing workspace..." && \
      RUST_BACKTRACE=full cargo test --no-run --verbose --workspace --all-targets
  RUN rustc --version --verbose | grep host && \
      du -sh /clap-rs_clap && \
      df -h
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
